Source Code

These source-code files derive from a printout of Luminary 116 (the Apollo 12 Lunar Module guidance computer program), from the personal library of original AGC developer Don Eyles, digitally photographed at archive.org, financially sponsored by Ron Burkey, and transcribed to source code by a team of volunteers. This colorized, syntax-highlighted form was created by assembling that transcribed source code. Note that the full page images are available on the Virtual AGC project page at archive.org, while reduced-size images are presented at the VirtualAGC project website. Report or fix any transcription errors at the Virtual AGC project code repository.

Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 116 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-071
	19:09 AUG. 11,1969
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

016436,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
016437,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
016438,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary revision 116.
016439,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM) 
016440,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 12.
016441,000007:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
016442,000008:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
016443,000009:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the
016444,000010:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
016445,000011:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 391-473
016446,000012:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
016447,000013:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.

016464,000030:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016465,000031:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
016466,000032:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
016467,000033:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016468,000034: 
016469,000035:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
016470,000036: 
016471,000037:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016472,000038:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016473,000039:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016474,000040:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016475,000041: 
016476,000042:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016477,000043:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016478,000044:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016479,000045:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016480,000046:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016481,000047: 
016482,000048:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016483,000049:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
016484,000050:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016485,000051:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
016486,000052: 
016487,000053:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
016488,000054:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
016489,000055: 
016490,000056:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES -
016491,000057: 
016492,000058:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
016493,000059:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016494,000060:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016495,000061:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016496,000062:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016497,000063: 
016498,000064:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
016499,000065:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
016500,000066:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016501,000067:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016502,000068: 
016503,000069:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016504,000070:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016505,000071:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016506,000072:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
016507,000073:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016508,000074: 
016509,000075:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
016510,000076: 
016511,000077:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
016512,000078:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
016513,000079:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 392 

016515,000081:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
016516,000082:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
016517,000083:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
016518,000084:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
016519,000085:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
016520,000086:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
016521,000087:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
016522,000088:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
016523,000089:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
016524,000090:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
016525,000091: 
016526,000092:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
016527,000093:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
016528,000094:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016529,000095: 
016530,000096:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
016531,000097: 
016532,000098:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
016533,000099:                                                                                                  #        IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
016534,000100:                                                                                                  #        ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
016535,000101: 
016536,000102:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
016537,000103:                                                                                                  #        IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
016538,000104:                                                                                                  #        (WITH OCTAL 01501).
016539,000105:                                                                                                  #        IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
016540,000106:                                                                                                  #        CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
016541,000107:                                                                                                  #                1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
016542,000108:                                                                                                  #                2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
016543,000109: 
016544,000110:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
016545,000111:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016546,000112: 
016547,000113:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
016548,000114: 
016549,000115:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
016550,000116:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL). :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
016551,000117:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
016552,000118:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
016553,000119: 
016554,000120:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION -
016555,000121: 
016556,000122:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
016557,000123:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
016558,000124:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
016559,000125:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
016560,000126: 
016561,000127:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 393 

016563,000129:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
016564,000130: 
016565,000131:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST -
016566,000132: 
016567,000133:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
016568,000134:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
016569,000135: 
016570,000136:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
016571,000137:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
016572,000138:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
016573,000139:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
016574,000140: 
016575,000141:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
016576,000142:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
016577,000143: 
016578,000144:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
016579,000145:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
016580,000146:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
016581,000147:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
016582,000148: 
016583,000149:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
016584,000150:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
016585,000151: 
016586,000152:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
016587,000153:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
016588,000154: 
016589,000155:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
016590,000156: 
016591,000157:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
016592,000158:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
016593,000159:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
016594,000160:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016595,000161: 
016596,000162:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
016597,000163:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016598,000164: 
016599,000165:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
016600,000166:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
016601,000167: 
016602,000168:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
016603,000169:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
016604,000170:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016605,000171: 
016606,000172:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING QUOTATION IS PROVIDED THROUGH THE COURTESY OF THE AUTHORS.
016607,000173: 
016608,000174:                                                                                                  #  ::IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT
016609,000175:                                                                                                  #  USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO

Page 394 

016611,000177:                                                                                                  #  CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
016612,000178:                                                                                                  #                                        HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
016613,000179: 
016614,000180:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
016615,000181: 
016616,000182:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016617,000183: 
016618,000184:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT      ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
016619,000185:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH      ERASE                   +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
016620,000186:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG       ERASE                   VERB CODE
016621,000187:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG       ERASE                   NOUN CODE
016622,000188:                                                                                                  #  XREG          ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
016623,000189:                                                                                                  #  YREG          ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
016624,000190:                                                                                                  #  ZREG          ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
016625,000191:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016626,000192:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016627,000193:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT      =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016628,000194:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
016629,000195:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016630,000196:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT      =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016631,000197:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
016632,000198:                                                                                                  #  MODREG        ERASE                   MODE CODE
016633,000199:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK       ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
016634,000200:                                                                                                  #  REQRET        ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
016635,000201:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
016636,000202:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS        ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
016637,000203:                                                                                                  #  NOUT          ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
016638,000204:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR      ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
016639,000205:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE       ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
016640,000206:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1      ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) = MONSAVE+1
016641,000207:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2      ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016642,000208:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB        ERASE           +13D    0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13, C RELAYS
016643,000209:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR      ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
016644,000210:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM        ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
016645,000211:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
016646,000212:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM      ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
016647,000213:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
016648,000214:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE      ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
016649,000215:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST       ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
016650,000216:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT      REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
016651,000217:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1       ERASE           +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
016652,000218:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2       ERASE           +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
016653,000219: 
016654,000220:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016655,000221: 
016656,000222:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016657,000223:

016660,000226:                                                                                                  #  DSEXIT        =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR DSPIN
016661,000227:                                                                                                  #  EXITEM        =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
016662,000228:                                                                                                  #  BLANKRET      =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR 2BLANK
016663,000229: 
016664,000230:                                                                                                  #  WRDRET        =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR 5BLANK
016665,000231:                                                                                                  #  WDRET         =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR DSPWD
016666,000232:                                                                                                  #  DECRET        =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)

016668,000234: 
016669,000235:                                                                                                  #  UPDATRET      =       POLISH          RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
016670,000236:                                                                                                  #  CHAR          =       POLISH          TEMP FOR CHARIN
016671,000237:                                                                                                  #  ERCNT         =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
016672,000238:                                                                                                  #  DECOUNT       =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
016673,000239: 
016674,000240:                                                                                                  #  SGNON         =       VBUF            TEMP FOR +,- ON
016675,000241:                                                                                                  #  NOUNTEM       =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
016676,000242:                                                                                                  #  DISTEM        =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERBS
016677,000243:                                                                                                  #  DECTEM        =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
016678,000244: 
016679,000245:                                                                                                  #  SGNOFF        =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR +,- ON
016680,000246:                                                                                                  #  NVTEMP        =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR NVSUB
016681,000247:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP1       =       VBUF    +1      STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART (=SFTEMP2-1)
016682,000248:                                                                                                  #  HITEMIN       =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016683,000249:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
016684,000250:                                                                                                  #  CODE          =       VBUF    +2      FOR DSPIN
016685,000251:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP2       =       VBUF    +2      STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART (=SFTEMP1+1)
016686,000252:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMIN       =       VBUF    +2      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016687,000253:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = HITEMIN+1.
016688,000254:                                                                                                  #  MIXTEMP       =       VBUF    +3      FOR MIXNOUN DATA
016689,000255:                                                                                                  #  SIGNRET       =       VBUF    +3      RETURN FOR +,- ON
016690,000256: 
016691,000257:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
016692,000258: 
016693,000259:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET        =       DOTINC          EXIT FROM ENTER
016694,000260:

016697,000263:

016699,000265:                                                                                                  #  MIXBR         =       MATINC          INDICATOR FOR MIXED OR NORMAL NOUN

016722,000288: 
016723,000289:                                                                                                  #  NNADTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
016724,000290:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
016725,000291:                                                                                                  #  IDAD1TEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016726,000292:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
016727,000293:                                                                                                  #  IDAD2TEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016728,000294:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.
016729,000295:                                                                                                  #  IDAD3TEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016730,000296:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
016731,000297:                                                                                                  #  RUTMXTEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN ONLY)
016732,000298: 
016733,000299:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016734,000300: 
016735,000301:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016736,000302: 
016737,000303:                                                                                                  #        MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
016738,000304:                                                                                                  #        BUF, +1, +2
016739,000305:                                                                                                  #        BUF2, +1, +2
016740,000306:                                                                                                  #        MPTEMP
016741,000307:                                                                                                  #        ADDRWD
016742,000308:                                                                                                  #  END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
016743,000309: 
016744,000310:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016745,000311: 
016746,000312:                                                                                                  #  DSPCNT        ERASE                   COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
016747,000313:                                                                                                  #  UPLOCK        ERASE                   BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
016748,000314:                                                                                                  #                                        RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
016749,000315:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION

016751,000317:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION

016757,000323:

Page 397 

016759,000325:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
016760,000326:                                                                                                  #  0             10000
016761,000327:                                                                                                  #  1             00001
016762,000328:                                                                                                  #  9             01001
016763,000329:                                                                                                  #  VERB          10001
016764,000330:                                                                                                  #  ERROR RES     10010
016765,000331:                                                                                                  #  KEY RLSE      11001
016766,000332:                                                                                                  #  +             11010
016767,000333:                                                                                                  #  -             11011
016768,000334:                                                                                                  #  ENTER         11100
016769,000335:                                                                                                  #  CLEAR         11110
016770,000336:                                                                                                  #  NOUN          11111
016771,000337: 
016772,000338:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
016773,000339:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
016774,000340:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
016775,000341:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
016776,000342:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
016777,000343:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016778,000344: 
016779,000345:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
016780,000346:                                                                                                  #  MD1   MD2                             (MAJOR MODE)
016781,000347:                                                                                                  #  VD1   VD2 (VERB)      ND1     ND2     (NOUN)
016782,000348:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  R1D2    R1D3    R1D4    R1D5    (R1)
016783,000349:                                                                                                  #  R2D1  R2D2    R2D3    R2D4    R2D5    (R2)
016784,000350:                                                                                                  #  R3D1  R3D2    R3D3    R3D4    R3D5    (R3)
016785,000351: 
016786,000352:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
016787,000353: 
016788,000354:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
016789,000355:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24              R2D2    10
016790,000356:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23              R2D3     7
016791,000357:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22              R2D4     6
016792,000358:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21              R2D5     5
016793,000359:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20              R3D1     4
016794,000360:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16              R3D2     3
016795,000361:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15              R3D3     2
016796,000362:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14              R3D4     1
016797,000363:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13              R3D5     0
016798,000364:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
016799,000365: 
016800,000366:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
016801,000367: 
016802,000368:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB        RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
016803,000369:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
016804,000370:                                                                                                  #  10            1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
016805,000371:                                                                                                  #  9             1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
016806,000372:                                                                                                  #  8             1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
016807,000373:                                                                                                  #  7             1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 398 

016809,000375:                                                                                                  #  6             0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
016810,000376:                                                                                                  #  5             0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
016811,000377:                                                                                                  #  4             0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
016812,000378:                                                                                                  #  3             0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
016813,000379:                                                                                                  #  2             0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
016814,000380:                                                                                                  #  1             0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
016815,000381:                                                                                                  #  0             0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
016816,000382:                                                                                                  #                0000        NO RELAYWORD

017238,000804:                                                                                                  #  ENTER PASS 0 IS THE EXECUTE FUNCTION. HIGHER ORDER ENTERS ARE TO LOAD
017239,000805:                                                                                                  #  DATA. THE SIGN OF REQRET DETERMINES THE PASS, + FOR PASS 0,- FOR HIGHER
017240,000806:                                                                                                  #  PASSES.
017241,000807: 
017242,000808:                                                                                                  #  MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED (MCTBS) NOUNS DESIRE AN ECADR TO BE LOADED
017243,000809:                                                                                                  #  WHEN USED WITH LOAD VERBS, MONITOR VERBS, OR DISPLAY VERBS (EXCEPT
017244,000810:                                                                                                  #  VERB = FIXED MEMORY DISPLAY, WHICH REQUIRES AN FCADR).

017529,001095:

Page 414 

017531,001097:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
017532,001098:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
017533,001099:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
017534,001100:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
017535,001101:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
017536,001102:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
017537,001103: 
017538,001104:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
017539,001105:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
017540,001106: 
017541,001107:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
017542,001108: 
017543,001109:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
017544,001110:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
017545,001111:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
017546,001112: 
017547,001113:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
017548,001114:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
017549,001115:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017550,001116:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
017551,001117:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017552,001118:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
017553,001119: 
017554,001120:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
017555,001121:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
017556,001122:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
017557,001123:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
017558,001124:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
017559,001125: 
017560,001126:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
017561,001127:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
017562,001128:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
017563,001129:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
017564,001130:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
017565,001131:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017566,001132:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
017567,001133:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017568,001134: 
017569,001135:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
017570,001136:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
017571,001137:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
017572,001138: 
017573,001139:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
017574,001140:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
017575,001141: 
017576,001142:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
017577,001143:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
017578,001144:

Page 415 

017580,001146:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS

018131,001697:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
018132,001698:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS. IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
018133,001699:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO .  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
018134,001700:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.

018160,001726:                                                                                                  #  TO EXECUTE  OF ORIGINAL LOAD VERB.  RECYCLE CAUSED BY  1) DECIMAL MACHINE

Page 439 

018728,002294:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
018729,002295:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
018730,002296:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
018731,002297:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
018732,002298:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
018733,002299: 
018734,002300:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
018735,002301:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
018736,002302:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
018737,002303:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
018738,002304:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
018739,002305:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
018740,002306:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
018741,002307: 
018742,002308:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
018743,002309:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018744,002310:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018745,002311: 
018746,002312:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
018747,002313:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
018748,002314: 
018749,002315:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
018750,002316:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
018751,002317: 
018752,002318:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

018877,002443:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
018878,002444:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
018879,002445:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
018880,002446:                                                                                                  #  
018881,002447:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
018882,002448: 
018883,002449:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
018884,002450:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
018885,002451:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
018886,002452: 
018887,002453:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
018888,002454:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
018889,002455:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
018890,002456: 
018891,002457: 41,3361           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
018892,002458: 41,3362           54776                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
018893,002459: 41,3363           31046                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
018894,002460: 41,3364           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
018895,002461: 41,3365           31016                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
018896,002462: 41,3366           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
018897,002463: 41,3367           03371                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
018898,002464: 41,3370           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

019321,002887: 
019322,002888:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019323,002889: 
019324,002890:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019325,002891: 
019326,002892:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019327,002893:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019328,002894:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019329,002895:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019330,002896: 
019331,002897:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019332,002898:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019333,002899:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019334,002900: 
019335,002901:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019336,002902:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019337,002903:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019338,002904:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019339,002905:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019340,002906:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019341,002907:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
019342,002908:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
019343,002909:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST. THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019344,002910:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019345,002911:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019346,002912: 
019347,002913: 40,3524           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019348,002914: 40,3525           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019349,002915: 40,3526           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019350,002916: 40,3527           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019351,002917: 40,3530           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019352,002918: 40,3531           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019353,002919: 40,3532           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019354,002920: 40,3533           03542                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019355,002921: 40,3534           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019356,002922: 40,3535           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019357,002923: 40,3536           03540                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019358,002924: 40,3537           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019359,002925: 40,3540           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019360,002926: 40,3541           21051                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019361,002927: 40,3542           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019362,002928: 40,3543           55011                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019363,002929: 40,3544           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019364,002930: 40,3545           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019365,002931: 40,3546           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019366,002932: 40,3547           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019367,002933: 
019368,002934: 40,3550                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019369,002935:

Page 453 

019371,002937:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
019372,002938:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019373,002939:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019374,002940:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019375,002941:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
019376,002942: 
019377,002943:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019378,002944:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS -
019379,002945:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
019380,002946: 
019381,002947:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019382,002948:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019383,002949: 
019384,002950:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019385,002951:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019386,002952:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019387,002953:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
019388,002954:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
019389,002955: 
019390,002956:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019391,002957:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019392,002958:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019393,002959:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019394,002960: 
019395,002961:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019396,002962:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
019397,002963:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019398,002964:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019399,002965:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019400,002966:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019401,002967:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
019402,002968: 
019403,002969:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019404,002970:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
019405,002971: 
019406,002972:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019407,002973:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
019408,002974: 
019409,002975:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019410,002976:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019411,002977: 
019412,002978:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
019413,002979:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019414,002980:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019415,002981:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
019416,002982:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019417,002983:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
019418,002984:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
019419,002985: 
019420,002986:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 454 

019422,002988:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019423,002989:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
019424,002990:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019425,002991:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019426,002992:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
019427,002993:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
019428,002994:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
019429,002995:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
019430,002996:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
019431,002997: 
019432,002998:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
019433,002999:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
019434,003000: 
019435,003001:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
019436,003002: 
019437,003003:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019438,003004:    4154           22007        NVSUB              LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019439,003005:    4155           54123        NVMONOPT           TS       NVTEMP                                
019440,003006:    4156           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019441,003007:    4157           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT

019541,003107:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS).
019542,003108:
