019544,003110:    4204                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019545,003111:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
019546,003112:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
019547,003113:    4205           55020                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
019548,003114:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
019549,003115:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019550,003116: 
019551,003117:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
019552,003118:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019553,003119:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019554,003120:                                                                                                  #                -0              DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
019555,003121:                                                                                                  #                        OR      RESEQUENCE      SET BY VERB 32
019556,003122: 
019557,003123:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
019558,003124:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
019559,003125:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
019560,003126:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019561,003127:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019562,003128:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
019563,003129:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
019564,003130:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
019565,003131:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
019566,003132:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
019567,003133: 
019568,003134:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 457 

019570,003136:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
019571,003137:                                                                                                  #  1)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
019572,003138:                                                                                                  #        EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019573,003139:                                                                                                  #  2)    DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
019574,003140:                                                                                                  #        NVSUBUSY.
019575,003141: 
019576,003142:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
019577,003143:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
019578,003144:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
019579,003145:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
019580,003146:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
019581,003147:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
019582,003148:    4215           55041                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
019583,003149:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019584,003150: 
019585,003151:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019586,003152: 
019587,003153:    4220           11041        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019588,003154:    4221           04227                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.

019629,003195:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
019630,003196:                                                                                                  #  CALL WITH BLANKING CODE IN A.

Page 465 

019913,003479:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
019914,003480: 
019915,003481:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019916,003482:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019917,003483:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019918,003484:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
019919,003485: 
019920,003486:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019921,003487:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1) BY ENDIDLE
019922,003488:                                                                                                  #                2) BY NVSUBUSY
019923,003489:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
019924,003490:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019925,003491:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019926,003492:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019927,003493: 
019928,003494:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019929,003495:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
019930,003496:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
019931,003497:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019932,003498:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019933,003499: 
019934,003500:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019935,003501:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019936,003502:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
019937,003503:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019938,003504:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019939,003505: 
019940,003506:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
019941,003507:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
019942,003508:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
019943,003509: 
019944,003510: 
019945,003511:                                                                                                  #  .
019946,003512: 
019947,003513:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
019948,003514:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
019949,003515:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
019950,003516:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019951,003517: 
019952,003518:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019953,003519:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
019954,003520:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
019955,003521:                                                                                                  #  1)    DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
019956,003522:                                                                                                  #        IS EXCEEDED.
019957,003523:                                                                                                  #  2)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 466 

019959,003525:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019960,003526: 
019961,003527:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
019962,003528:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
019963,003529:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
019964,003530:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
019965,003531:    4443           10631                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
019966,003532:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
019967,003533: 
019968,003534:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
019969,003535:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
019970,003536: 
019971,003537: 04,2631                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
019972,003538: 04,2631                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019973,003539: 04,2631           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
019974,003540: 04,2632           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019975,003541: 04,2633           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
019976,003542: 04,2634           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
019977,003543: 04,2635           30001                           CA       L                                     
019978,003544: 04,2636           55042                           TS       DSPLIST                               
019979,003545: 04,2637           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019980,003546: 
019981,003547:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
019982,003548:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
019983,003549:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
019984,003550:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
019985,003551:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
019986,003552: 
019987,003553:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
019988,003554:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019989,003555:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019990,003556:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
019991,003557:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019992,003558:    4450           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019993,003559:    4451           61011                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
019994,003560:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019995,003561:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
019996,003562:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
019997,003563:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.

020153,003719:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
020154,003720:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
020155,003721:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
020156,003722:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
020157,003723:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
020158,003724:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
020159,003725:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
